A coastal ship has run aground off the coast of Scotland and sent out a distress signal. Lifeboats have been sent to rescue it. Another Belgian ship has also run aground, and another ship has sunk, but its crew members have been rescued.

National News Agency, Paris, 23rd - The losses of French fishing boats on the Atlantic coast during this storm are the greatest ever seen. Currently, there are still 500 missing, and casualties are estimated to be in the hundreds. Although torpedo boats are searching the English Channel and the Atlantic coast, progress is greatly hindered by the heavy fog. The French cabinet is now planning to allocate a large amount of money for relief.

Japanese Army Ministry Firmly Rejects Savings 63

Budget Preparation Becomes More Difficult

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 24th - Army military and political reform was one of the ten political programs declared by the Minsei Party when it formed the cabinet. Now that a year has passed since the cabinet was formed, neither an investigation committee has been established nor any substantive plan has been obtained. Moreover, when the 1931 budget was being prepared, it was expected that revenue would decrease by 130 million yuan, and it was extremely difficult to fill the gap. Minister of Finance Inoue decided to uniformly reduce the established expenses of various ministries according to the rate of price decline, and also intended to require the army to save 20 to 30 million yuan in the established expenses of the budget. However, the Army Ministry has firmly refused. The government has not solved the difficulties with the navy, and has also had a disagreement with the army. It is worth noting that one wave has not subsided and another has risen again.

Domestic News

The Process of Liaoning and Zhang's Announcement of Circular Telegrams 64

Two armies have been organized to take over defense of Peiping and Tientsin

Shenyang Correspondence: Some days ago, Zhang Xueliang, upon his return to Shenyang from Beidaihe, immediately telegraphed the leading figures of the northeastern provinces and regions, ordering them to gather in Shenyang within a limited time to attend a cadre meeting to discuss the policies for dealing with the current situation. This was because the Northeast's current position had implications of utmost importance both domestically and internationally. For several months, representatives from various parties had been traveling back and forth, causing much difficulty in dealing with them. Moreover, the floating public opinions and rumors fabricated by foreign newspapers were enough to affect social security. Therefore, in order to stabilize public sentiment and avoid the entanglement of lobbying representatives, it was decided to issue a circular telegram to express his attitude. On the 15th, leading figures from various provinces and regions, such as Zhang Zuoxiang, Tang Yulin, Wan Fulin, and Zhang Jinghui, had arrived at the Beiling Villa one after another. The cadre meeting was immediately convened to carefully study and discuss the matter. As a result, it was decided to adhere to the Dongdian (Eastern Telegram) proposal, calling on all parties to cease hostilities. The draft telegram was prepared by Wang Shuhan, the secretary-general of the Chief Executive's Office, on the 15th. For the sake of prudence, it was meticulously studied and revised until the 18th before it was decided to send it out. During this period, the draft telegram was once sent to the telegraph office on the 17th but was later withdrawn for delayed release. It was not until 7:30 AM on the 18th that it was sent to the telegraph office again and officially released (note that the text of the telegram has already been published in previous reports). Although this circular telegram was only sent on the 18th, the decision had been made several days earlier. Although the wording may have been revised, the general outline remained largely unchanged. The representative of Yan Xishan stationed in Shenyang received the news on the 15th and immediately telegraphed Yan, who then issued a telegram announcing his retirement. After the telegram was issued, representatives from the North, seeing that the Northeast authorities had made a clear statement, had no room to maneuver in staying in Shenyang. Kong Fanwei took the No. 102 train of the Beining Railway at 9:45 AM on the 18th to return to Peiping and then to Shijiazhuang. Jia Jingde and Xue Dubi also left Shenyang for the customs on the morning of the 19th. Currently, the Jin army in the Peiping and Tientsin areas has begun to withdraw. Due to the urging of various parties, the Northeast has decided to send troops to the customs immediately to peacefully take over the defense. The troops currently being prepared are organized into two army corps. The first army is commanded by Yu Xuezhong, the commander of Yuguan, and its subordinate units are the 23rd Infantry Brigade stationed in Yuguan (formerly Ma Tingfu's troops) and the 27th Brigade stationed in Lulong (Liu Naichang's troops), and the 1st Cavalry Division stationed in Liushouying (Zheng Zesheng's troops). The second army is commanded by Wang Shuchang, the director of the Military Affairs Department of the Border Defense Command, and its subordinate units are the 4th Brigade stationed in Xingcheng (Liu Yifei's troops), the 2nd Brigade stationed in Dahushan (Ding Xichun's troops), and the 25th Brigade stationed in Gaoqiao (Yao Dongfan's troops). In addition to the First Army Headquarters being organized at the discretion of Commander Yu Xuezhong, the organization of the Second Army Headquarters is entirely staffed by personnel transferred from the Border Defense Command. Chen Qinruo, the deputy director of the Military Affairs Department of the Border Defense Command, has been appointed as the Chief of Staff of the Second Army, and Wang Dexin, the chief of the First Section of the Military Affairs Department, has been appointed as the Director of the Staff Office. Liu Mingyun has been appointed as the Director of the Adjutant Office. Other military officers and adjutants of the army headquarters are being appointed and dispatched in succession in recent days. They will enter the customs in the coming days. As for the military station, which is related to the march of the army, the Sixth Section of the Border Defense Command has been tasked with the responsibility of preparing it. It has been decided that the general station will be located in Shanhaiguan, and the warehouse will be located in Huanggu Tun. Two sub-stations will be set up to accompany the first and second armies to handle the food and supplies for the personnel and horses. Wang Lie has been appointed as the chief of the general station, and Wen Runfang has been appointed as the deputy chief. They have started setting up the station since the 17th. Gao Jiyi, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, has been ordered to go to Shanhaiguan on the evening of the 18th to coordinate military transportation. The sale of tickets for the through train between Peiping and Shenyang has been suspended since the afternoon of the 19th, and only tickets to Leizhou are being sold. It is reported that Yu Xuezhong's troops have advanced towards Leizhou and will be waiting for orders in Junliangcheng. In the future, the first and second armies will take Peiping and Tientsin as their destinations. The first army will take over the defense of Peiping, and the second army will take over the defense of Tientsin. (19th)

The Circumstances of the Northeast Sending Troops to Peiping and Tientsin 65

Zhang Xueliang Advocated an Early Decision in Beidaihe

The Reasons Why the Yan and Feng Factions Misunderstood Zhang's Telegram

Tientsin Correspondence: Since the Yan and Feng factions initiated the war, the conflict has lasted for six months. After Yan's defeat and return from the Jinpu Railway, he sought to replenish military funds by issuing banknotes of the Zhonghua National Bank on a large scale. Many merchants dared not accept them, and larger stores closed down on various pretexts. Recently, the banknotes of the Shanxi Provincial Bank have fallen to 60% of their face value, causing social and economic chaos. Therefore, the people of the North are extremely eager for a quick end to the war and place their hopes on Zhang Xueliang, who can sway the situation with a single move. In fact, Zhang Xueliang's policy and plan for using troops against the Yan and Feng factions had already been decided during his stay in Beidaihe. According to key members of Zhang's staff, the meetings after Zhang's return to Shenyang were merely discussions on the deployment of troops and the strategy of warfare. After Zhang Zuoxiang and others arrived, the entire plan for using troops was finalized. The 16th was the wedding day of Zhang Zuoxiang's son. While everyone in Shenyang was congratulating him, Zhang Xueliang personally drafted the mobilization plan and deployment orders, appointing Yu Xuezhong as the commander of the First Army, with the four mixed brigades under Liu Naichang, Yao Dongfan, Li Zhentang, and Zhao Zhixiang as the advance troops, and adding the two brigades under Liu Yifei and Dong Yingbin. Yu Xuezhong, the commander of the First Army to take over the defense of Peiping and Tientsin, was to have his troops embark on trains at Shanhaiguan and other defensive areas on the 19th, and occupy Tientsin by the early morning of the 21st. When this reporter drafted this letter, he thought that the army was already preparing. Gao Jiyi, the director of the Beining Railway Bureau, personally coordinated the transportation of the troops. Several days ago, he secretly transferred vehicles from within the customs to outside the customs, assembling over 800 vehicles. It is said that 13 trains were used for Yu's troops to depart. Gao Jiyi has arrived in Shanhaiguan and is scheduled to come to Tientsin with the army. It is also reported that Wu Tiecheng, a representative of the Central Government, will also come to Tientsin with the army, while Zhang Qun will temporarily stay in Shenyang as the supervisor for Zhang Xueliang when he takes the post of deputy commander of the army, navy, and air force. After occupying Tientsin, Yu's army will simultaneously advance towards Peiping and recover the entire territory of Hebei. Zhang Xueliang also appointed Wang Shuchang as the commander of the Second Army and Hu Yukun as the commander of the Third Army. After Yu's troops occupy Peiping and Tientsin, he will order Wang and Hu to lead their troops into the customs and advance towards the Jinpu and Pinghan lines, with the aim of completely eliminating the Yan and Feng forces. It is said that the Yan army is now preparing to retreat.

Zhang Xueliang's telegram arrived in Tientsin on the evening of the 18th and was initially detained by the Jin army. After reading it among themselves, they all thought that the wording was peaceful and did not contain any clear accusations against the Jin side. They all believed that Zhang was merely expressing his opinion on the current situation, similar to the nature of the Dongdian he issued in March. The next morning, it was distributed to various newspapers for publication. After receiving the telegram, a certain newspaper discussed it with the Jin side, who said that it could be published. Therefore, it was published in the newspaper on the 19th. It is said that the Jin side had always mistakenly believed that Zhang had a good impression of them and never expected that his telegram would be followed by the arrival of a powerful army. After Zhang's telegram arrived in Tientsin, the Peiping and Tientsin press simultaneously received a telegram from Yan, which roughly stated that the central air force had repeatedly dropped bombs and that he was willing to retreat in order to save the people's lives. This telegram came after Zhang's telegram, so it was generally concluded that it was a prelude to Yan's resignation. However, if Peiping and Tientsin were occupied by the Northeast Army, even if he wanted to resign, there would be no place for him to do so.

As for why the Yan and Feng factions had always believed that the Northeast would not resort to military force against them, there were two reasons: one was the subtlety of the Northeast's handling of the situation, and the other was the failure of the representatives of the Yan and Feng factions to ascertain the other party's true intentions. It is said that Jia Jingde and Xue Dubi were ordered to go to Shenyang, and it was not until the third day after their arrival that they were able to meet with Zhang. After meeting, they did not first inquire about Zhang's intentions, but instead ramblingly stated that Yan hoped that the Northeast would participate in the new government, and that Zhang Zuoxiang, Zhang Jinghui, and others could be given positions as government commissioners and ministers, with the number of positions to be decided by the Northeast. They tried to use the positions of commissioners and ministers as bait. Zhang listened with great displeasure and did not say a word in reply. Jia and Xue left without understanding his intentions. The second meeting was at Zhang's public banquet for representatives from various parties. Apart from polite conversation, no substantive matters were discussed. The last meeting was after Zhang issued the telegram. They merely explained the meaning of peace to them and asked them to report back to their masters. Therefore, they never understood Zhang's true intentions. (September 19)

Jinpu Railway Luokou Iron Bridge to be Repaired 66

Central Army to Cross the River and Pursue the Enemy Within Days

Jinan Correspondence: The battle situation on the Longhai and Pinghan lines has taken a sharp turn for the worse in recent days. On the Jinpu Line, the enemy troops on the opposite bank of Luokou have also loaded supplies and ammunition onto trains and are transporting them to Dezhou in preparation for retreat. The Central Army will cross the river and pursue the enemy within two or three days. Han Fuju, the commander-in-chief of the First Army Corps, has sent Wei Jinglu, the captain of the second team of the first battalion of the second transportation corps, to expedite the transport of the materials originally unloaded from the Luokou Bridge from Nanjing, and has appointed Wei to be responsible for planning the repair of the bridge with Hu Shenghong, an engineer from the Jinpu Railway. Currently, the iron bridge materials have been transported to Yanzhou Station and will arrive in Jinan in the next day or two. It is reported that engineer Hu plans to request the Nanjing Railway Bureau to allocate more materials in addition to the materials that were originally unloaded, as it is not easy to find a solution for those destroyed by the Jin army. According to Mr. Hu, if the materials are available, the bridge can be repaired within two or three days. The Central Army's crossing of the river to pursue the enemy is expected to occur within three to five days. (September 22)

Zhu Mao Peng Huang Fled from Hunan to Jiangxi 67

The Communist Party Still Attempts to Invade Nanxun

The 18th Division Advances from Tongwan to Suppress the Communists

All Sectors Petition the Central Government for Troops

Nanchang Correspondence: The Communist bandits Zhu, Mao, Peng, Huang, Lin, and Li and their respective forces, under the orders of the Third International, intend to seize political power in Hunan and Jiangxi. However, since their defeat in Changsha, they have shown signs of fleeing towards Jiangxi. According to reliable military sources, the Communist bandits are fleeing into Jiangxi in two routes. Peng and Huang's bogus Fourth Army is entering the Zhutan Bridge area of Wanzai via Pingliu, only dozens of miles away from Wancheng. Zhu and Mao's bogus Third Army is heading towards Yuanzhou and Shanggao via Lizhuping (Xiang) and Lian (Hua), with the intention of advancing towards Nanxun. However, since the Communist bandits retreated into Hunan, this province has been closely guarded. Currently, there are four or five regiments of the 18th Division on the border between Hunan and Jiangxi. Brigade Commander Dai, believing that the mountainous terrain of Wanzai is not suitable for combat, has concentrated his troops in the Shanggao, Yuanzhou, and Gaoan areas to lure the bandits deep into the area so that they can be wiped out on the plains. All the strategic locations in Yuanzhou, Shanggao, and Gaoan have trenches and defensive fortifications. However, when the 104th Regiment withdrew from Wanzai, the residents, unable to stop them from leaving, cried bitterly and followed the army with their elderly and children. In addition to sending personnel to Wuhan to consult with Director He about the plan for attack and defense and requesting that the Fourth Army and the Gongluo Divisions enter Jiangxi to assist in the suppression of the bandits, the Ninth Army Headquarters is also continuing to carry out defensive works in the provincial capital. Temporary command posts have been set up for the outer trenches (outside the electrified fence) and earthworks near the provincial capital. Yu Zizun, the battalion commander of the 18th Division's engineering battalion, is responsible for the area west of Zhangjiang, including the Niuhang Station. Wang Ge, the chief of the First Section of the provincial government, is responsible for the earthworks in the old urban area east of Zhangjiang. Each household in the city is assigned two workers to rush to build day and night. More than twenty blockhouses are planned to be built near Nanchang, each three zhang high and four zhang long and four zhang wide, built with bricks and cement. Moreover, more than ten locations, including Shengmi (30 li from the province) upstream of the Gan River, Qilijie downstream, Niuhang Station on the Nanxun Road, and Liantang on the Nanzhang Highway, are also being contracted to build blockhouses, which can be completed soon. Once these blockhouses are completed, the firepower can reach more than 100 li. Even if the Communist bandits are cunning, they will not be able to succeed.

Some days ago, General Commander Lu received a large batch of bullets from the Nanjing General Headquarters and a map of the three provinces suppressing the bandits from the Wuhan Headquarters, which were successively distributed to various departments yesterday. At the same time, multiple copies of Zhu De's photo were printed and ordered to be strictly investigated by his subordinates. Due to the tense situation of Zhu and Mao fleeing to Jiangxi, all sectors in this province, in addition to the General Chamber of Commerce sending a telegram to General Commander Chiang requesting that the two brigades of the 50th Division on the front line be transferred back, the instructors of the industrial, commercial, and academic groups in this city also held a joint meeting at the city government on the 22nd to discuss ways to request troops. It was decided to send a telegram to General Commander Chiang and Director He requesting that several more divisions be dispatched to Jiangxi immediately to avoid repeating the mistakes of Hunan and causing the people to suffer. At the same time, they also telegraphed Liu Zhi and Xiong Shihui to request that they forward their request to the Central Government on their behalf to save the critical situation. (September 23)

Wuhan Headquarters Organizes Propaganda Brigade 68

Expand Anti-Communist Propaganda in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi

Hankou Correspondence: He Yingqin, the director of the Wuhan Headquarters, recently received a telegram from the Central Government stating that the 104th Standing Committee of the Central Committee resolved that the Communist bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are rampant and that during this period of suppression, a propaganda brigade should be organized to expose the crimes of the Communist Party as much as possible. After receiving the order, Mr. He immediately began preparations and appointed Liu Guang as the brigade commander, ordering him to organize the brigade and set off for propaganda as soon as possible. Today (22nd), he started working in the Wuhan Military, Police, and Academic Research Association and will set off for Changsha and then Jiangxi to carry out his work. Today, the first brigade affairs meeting was held and several cases were decided. It has been learned that the organization and work plan of the brigade are as follows:

Organization Overview: The brigade is currently provisionally divided into three detachments, each with one detachment leader and seven propagandists. Wu Yue is the leader of the first detachment, Li Zhizhuo is the leader of the second detachment, and Cheng Shuofu is the leader of the third detachment. On the 22nd, Liu Guang, the brigade commander of the brigade, presented a request to the headquarters to add more propagandists, who will be selected from the graduates of the political science department of the military academy. 19 of them have already arrived in Hankou, and the rest are also students from the third term of Whampoa and later, who will hold various positions.

Work Plan: The brigade is divided into three detachments. It was originally planned to station one detachment in each of the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi. However, because the Communist atmosphere in Hunan is the most rampant and the propaganda work is also more important, it has been decided that the entire brigade will set off for Changsha first. The brigade headquarters will temporarily follow the headquarters of the Fourth Route Army, and each detachment will set off with the Communist suppression troops. In the recovered areas, they will comfort the people and explain the Communist Party's conspiracies and crimes to the masses. At the same time, they will also be responsible for training soldiers. After most of the Communist bandits in Hunan are suppressed, they will work in Liling, Youxian, Liuyang, and Pingjiang, and then transfer to Xiushui, Tonggu, and Wanzai in Jiangxi for propaganda. As for Hubei, because the Communist Party's power is weak and the garrison troops are strong, it is easy to suppress them, so the propaganda work will be postponed. (September 22)

Liaoning Province Seals Up French Merchant Machine Factory 69

Due to the Factory's Repeated Resistance to Orders and Private Manufacture of Firearms

Shenyang Correspondence: The French merchant Feilong Machine Factory was previously found by our side to be privately manufacturing firearms. The Liaoning Special Commissioner's Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs negotiated with the French Consul and ordered the factory to stop work on the 12th of last month. However, the factory manager, Bao Keshu, outwardly complied but inwardly disobeyed. On the 16th of this month, he gathered many craftsmen at the factory to resume work and privately manufacture rifles. This was discovered by the Commercial Port Public Security First Bureau, which immediately sent police to the factory to stop them and arrest the craftsmen. The craftsmen at the factory, upon seeing this, immediately jumped over the wall and escaped. Only Wang Yao, a supplier of gunpowder, was caught. According to his confession, he was forced to work by Bao Keshu. More than ten newly manufactured rifles were found in the factory. After receiving the report from the Public Security Bureau, the Foreign Affairs Office immediately lodged a serious protest with the French Consul. It also went to the provincial capital with the Public Security Bureau and sent police to seal the factory at 4:00 PM on the 17th. All the public and private debts owed by the factory to the Chinese side must still be negotiated with the French Consul for repayment. As for the large batch of firearms hidden by the factory in Laoguabao, after the Shenyang County Public Security Bureau was ordered to inspect and seize them, the Military Affairs Office of the Chief Executive's Office ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly monitor them and wait for disposal. It is now reported that the authorities intend to confiscate the firearms. (September 19)

Local Correspondence Songjiang 71

The Township Chief of the Tenth District Kidnapped: Shen Renru, the township chief of Xiaogang Township in the tenth district of the county, has a family that is not particularly wealthy but can barely make ends meet. However, he was coveted by bandits. At 12:00 on the night of the 18th, more than a dozen bandits speaking the local Hakka dialect suddenly came with guns and broke into his house. They dispersed into various rooms and ransacked them, causing considerable losses. Before leaving, they kidnapped Shen Renru, escorted him onto a bandit boat, and took the loot westward. It is said that before leaving, the bandits told his family that they would have to pay 2,000 yuan for his ransom. The district chief has reported this to the county government and requested that the bandits be apprehended and the hostage rescued.

60% of District Administrative Expenses Granted: The county government previously received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs to reduce the administrative expenses of the district offices, stating that the administrative expenses should not exceed one-third of the original budget. The county government allocated the surtax in accordance with the instructions of the Department. All the district chiefs presented the difficult situation of the district's heavy administrative burden to the county government and requested to maintain the original situation. After discussion at the 63rd county administration meeting, the county government decided to allocate 60% of the original budget and submitted it to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval. It is now learned that the Department has instructed that Jin County Chief has wired the First District to inform all districts to comply. From September, the monthly administrative expenses for Grade C districts will be 150 yuan, and for Grade D districts, it will be 120 yuan.

Changshu 72

Young Woman Commits Suicide Due to Inability to Endure Abuse: Gu Zhenxiang, the second son of Gu Shiqing of Dong Taiping Lane in this county town, is currently studying at Jinling University in Nanjing and will graduate next year. Zhenxiang married Cai Dehua (22 years old), the daughter of Cai Yunkang from the same county, as his wife last winter. The couple's love for each other was very deep after their marriage. Gu and Cai originally married out of free love. However, Zhenxiang's mother, Xu, was very opposed to this. Since Cai entered the door, the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law had disagreements. Xu often interfered with her daughter-in-law's actions. Whenever Dehua had something to go out, Xu would order her younger daughter, Liwen (currently studying at the Zhihe Midwifery School), to secretly follow her, fearing that she would do something out of line. She also often received scolding from her aunt-in-law. As a result, Dehua was depressed and had long harbored the idea of committing suicide. She had sent valuable items and jewelry to her own mother to wait for a later day. The other day (the 21st), she was scolded by her aunt-in-law for some unknown reason. She secretly went out to buy two bottles of sleeping pills and several boxes of Red Head Matches. She swallowed the sleeping pills on the way, crying as she walked, and suddenly encountered two patrol officers, Zhou Shousong and Li Yongsheng, of the Fourth Sub-Precinct near the entrance of Taiping Lane. The patrol officers saw that she had a depressed look on her face and asked her what was wrong. Dehua did not answer, but threw the small bottle into the trash can and left. The patrol officers knew that something was wrong and used a flashlight to shine on the trash can and discovered the small bottle of sleeping pills and a visiting card. Because the police station was near the Gu family and he was familiar with Cai Dehua, the patrol officer immediately went to the Gu family to report. Her father-in-law, Gu Shiqing, did not pay attention at the time. After Dehua returned home, she wrote two letters of suicide, one to her husband and one to her parents, instructing them to pay off the debts of the various stores and attach the 500 yuan passbook of the Bank of China to her mother. After finishing writing, she swallowed eight boxes of matches and went to sleep. The next morning (the 23rd), when Dehua was seen, her face and limbs were showing signs of abnormality. She was called but did not respond. Sleeping pills were found on the table, and it was known that she had committed suicide by taking poison. A Western doctor was called for emergency treatment. He said that she had taken too much poison and that her life was in danger. Currently, Cai's family has negotiated with the Gu family and telegraphed to Beijing to invite her husband, Zhenxiang, to return home to find a solution.

Suzhou 73

Another Robbery Case in Hengjing: Six bandits armed with single knives and other weapons suddenly came to Hengjing Shilubang the other night. They used bamboo poles to prop themselves into the home of farmer He Shenkang and tied up He, his wife Zhou, and their neighbor Zhang Kunlin. They threatened and injured Zhou's right shoulder and searched for an hour, robbing clothes and ornaments worth 4-500 yuan before leaving with a howl. After the county government expanded the report, it has been ordered to pursue and apprehend the bandits.

The Sutra Chanting Donation is Temporarily Maintained: The county government previously received an order from the provincial government to stop collecting the Sutra Chanting Donation. The Education and Finance Bureaus requested that the collection of the Sutra Chanting Donation be temporarily continued because it was a designated special fund for education and there were no designated replacement taxes.

Wuxi 74

Another Robbery Case Reported in Tuntian Village: Xu Peixiu, a villager in Tunshiangsang Village near Shitouzhen, a small prosperous village in the Fifth District (Tianshang City), is a farmer who lives a modest life. However, at 12:00 the other night, more than a dozen bandits speaking the local dialect and armed with air guns, knives, clubs, and flashlights broke into his house. They dragged Xu Peixiu and others out of bed, tied them up with ropes, and then ransacked the house at will, looting for an hour before carrying the loot away. After the incident, it was checked and found that 153 yuan in paper money, as well as leather wallets, clothes, gold and silver jewelry, etc., were robbed, totaling more than 1,000 yuan in losses. Dozens of field deeds were also robbed. Yesterday, the victim Xu Peixiu and the head of the village, Pan Wenyin, reported to the county government and requested that the police be sent to investigate and recover the stolen goods.

Prisoners Attempt to Escape from the County Jail Unsuccessfully: Prison guard Xia Xueqin found the other day that four prisoners in rooms 1 and 2, Zhu Jinsheng (not yet sentenced), Zhang Aiyi (sentenced to seven years), Shen Yunqing (eight years, transferred from Shanghai for confinement), and Cai Heyuan (seven years), were digging a tunnel under the floorboards of Cai's room in an attempt to escape through the prison wall. He immediately ordered the police to strictly confine the above-mentioned prisoners and telegraphed County Chief Pan to inform the trial office. Trial Officers Zhou and Yu led the police to inspect the scene and found a tunnel dug under the floorboards of the room, with a small knife and a spatula left next to the tunnel. After questioning, it was clarified that the prisoners had been working at night for five days and used the floorboards to cover the tunnel during the day. Fortunately, three days ago, Gong Jinbao, Chen Shenggu, Yun Jinsheng, and other sick prisoners in the same room reported to the head and deputy directors of the guards, Wang Weizheng and He Shaolin. After detailed investigation and strict precautions, the escape was unsuccessful. Zhou and Yu then interrogated all the above-mentioned people and the four prisoners, Zhu, Zhang, Shen, and Cai. They then ordered the four prisoners, Zhu, etc., to be shackled with large double shackles, confined separately, and closely monitored while awaiting legal proceedings.

Record of a Serial Robbery and Murder Case: Near Nan Shuangmiao Town in the Fifteenth District: Zhou Haojin (also known as Zhou Renbao) and his brother Zhou Genbao were robbed and shot to death. Zhou Haojin's son, Xuechen, was also shot and killed, and Zhou Haojin and Genbao were injured. The two families were robbed of about 300 yuan. After the incident, the victim reported to the county government. Lu Yijie, a member of the case-clearing committee, opened a court and clarified that Zhou Genbao had received a hundred yuan in subscription fees on the day of the robbery, and that Chen Fuquan, the brother-in-law of the head subscriber, Zhu Peisheng, also wanted to receive the money, but it was not allowed. Zhang then harbored resentment and robbed them. Therefore, Zhang was very suspicious. He requested detention of the case. Yesterday, Supervising Trial Officer Yu and the police went to the countryside to investigate and found that Zhou Xuechen had been shot in a vital part and died, Zhou Genbao's injuries were still minor, and Zhou Haojin's leg bone had been broken by a bullet and his injuries were very serious. Zhu Peisheng and Zhang Fuquan were immediately detained for interrogation. After a thorough interrogation, Zhu Peisheng was ordered to post bail, and Zhang Fuquan was detained pending investigation.

Four Bandits Apprehended and Sent to the District: Bandits Wang Xiaogou, Hang Heshang, Ma Hongchu, etc., had previously repeatedly gathered crowds to rob Dongfang Bridge, Xinhe Bridge, and Fenshuidun and other places. Recently, the bandits sneaked to Xueyanqiao Town, which is located on the border between Wuxi and Changshu, intending to rob. Wu Zongjie, the commander of the town's defense corps, discovered this and immediately led the troops to search everywhere. They captured four bandits, Wang Xiaogou, Hang Heshang, Ma Hongchu, and Chen Jinquan, in the vicinity. They were immediately escorted to the Second District Water Police. Yesterday, Captain Chen Rongquan of the Sixth Team opened a court for interrogation. Wang, Hang, and Ma confessed to repeatedly gathering crowds to rob them. However, Chen Jinquan firmly denied it. After the interrogation, they were ordered to be detained and await the arrest of the other fugitives before being transferred to the county for interrogation.

Changzhou 75

Robbery and Injury in Zangcunzhen: On the evening of the 23rd, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived in Zangcunzhen, a town bordering the four counties of Yixing, Liyang, Jintan, and Wujin in the southern countryside of Wuyi. They carried machine guns and Mauser pistols, first firing shots to intimidate, and then proceeded to rob the Tong Shengtang Pharmacy, Zhen Taifeng Rice Shop, Heng Changsheng Dried Goods Store, Guang Sheng Beijing-Guang Goods Store, and the Orchid Shop opened by Chuyushan, incurring heavy losses for each business. Ju, a shop assistant at Tong Shengtang Pharmacy, was shot in the back while fleeing and fell to the ground. After the robbery, the bandits headed towards Butouzhen.

Bankruptcy of Changfeng Bean Shop: The Changfeng Bean Shop outside the West Gate of Wuyi, established by Gu Quansheng and others with Zhang Shou Kang as manager, has been in operation for two years. It suddenly went bankrupt the day before yesterday. News today (24th) indicates a total loss of over 30,000 yuan in deposits and over 10,000 yuan in customer goods. All creditors are in a state of panic. Zhang Shou Kang and others have gone into hiding and cannot be found. They are currently gathering to discuss methods of pursuing compensation.

Jiashan 76

Tax Collection Leads to Market Strike by Money Dealers: On the 23rd, the county government received a report that the money dealers in Xitang had gone on strike, causing significant impact. It dispatched officials to mediate. The reason was the continued payment of 40% of the assigned customs tax coupon quota, but Commissioner Zeng of the county government suddenly arrested the six Zhuang Xieli (representatives in charge of negotiations) and sent them to the Public Security Bureau, arousing public anger and leading to a general strike. After mediation, an agreement was reached to pay another 20%, and they agreed to comply. All markets reopened in the afternoon.

Jiaxing 77

Anti-Bandit Headquarters Intercepts Bandit Boats: Hang Yi, the anti-bandit commander of Jiahu, considering that Taozhuang, Tianningzhuang, Youchegang and other towns in Jiaxing and Jiashan had been repeatedly plundered by bandits, previously joined forces with Xu, the district chief of the Second District Water Police, to lead a team to suppress them. They intercepted a large number of bandit boats and rescued many hostages, obtaining a lot of stolen goods, weapons, etc. As Commander Hang believed that the bandits had not been completely eradicated and were closely related to the security of various towns in the northern countryside, he again supervised the troops in mid-September and, together with District Chief Xu, set out on the warship Zhiguo to patrol the border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. While patrolling, they discovered bandit traces in the Zhujia River area at the border of Wujiang and Qingpu counties in Jiangsu province. They encountered sixteen bandit boats there and opened fire, engaging in a fierce battle for a long time, killing more than twenty bandits, capturing three alive, and intercepting thirteen bandit boats and nine guns. They also rescued three hostages. The remaining bandits and three bandit boats had already escaped during the fierce battle, so they were not intercepted. The intercepted bandit boats, bandits, guns, hostages, etc., were brought to He on the 23rd for processing.

Yangzhou 78

Confiscated Copper Coins Not Yet Released: The case of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau's First Branch intercepting twenty carts of copper coins outside Quekoucheng has already been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the copper coins have not yet been resolved because the reporter, Wei Lidun, has repeatedly proved that the copper coins were indeed smuggled to Shanghai, while the Chamber of Commerce has presented various counter-arguments, believing that they were definitely not smuggled. The county government, taking the matter seriously, ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate in detail. It is said that although the director of the Public Security Bureau has confirmed that the copper coins were not for export, the county government still fears that this is not true, so yesterday (22nd) it instructed the bureau to re-investigate and verify.

Large Quantity of Opium Discovered: Captain Wei of the county police brigade, acting on a confidential tip, believed that a certain family on Jiajian Bridge in the city was hiding a large quantity of opium. Yesterday (22nd) afternoon at 6:00 pm, he selected twelve members of the Mauser pistol squad and went to the address. They indeed found hundreds of taels of opium, one opium dealer, and one handgun, as well as opium paraphernalia, which were all detained and sent to the court for legal action. However, it is said that the opium dealer has a significant background, and he is currently seeking assistance from powerful figures to lobby the county government, the brigade headquarters, and the county court for an exemption. However, whether this will be effective remains unknown.

Nantong 79

Bandit Jin Lezhu Executed by Firing Squad in Yiyu: Bandit Cui Huang, also known as Jin Lezhu, committed numerous crimes and fled to Shanghai. The county government sent police to Shanghai to escort him back to Tong and handed him over to the Anti-Bandit Headquarters. After interrogation, he was taken to Yiyu and executed by firing squad.

District Chief's Corruption and Extortion Case Returned to Judicial Review: After Lu Jianqu and others accused Guanren District Chief He Wenqiu of corruption and extortion, County Magistrate Liu presented the case to the Department of Civil Affairs, requesting that another qualified district chief be appointed to replace him. The case was transferred to the county court for review.

The Bandit Situation in Tong, Ru, Tai, and Jing is Gradually Calming: Bandits and communists are rampant in the four counties of Tong, Ru, Tai, and Jing north of the Yangtze River. The bandits call themselves the Fourteenth Army of the Red Army. After being encircled and suppressed by the provincial security forces, the pseudo-army was defeated. On one hand, they used surrendered bandits and communists to unearth hidden weapons. Currently, the bandit situation is gradually calming, and the Yang and Zhou battalions are dividing roads to search for the defeated bandits.

Lishui 80

Agricultural and Mining Department Sends Commissioners to Inspect Afforestation Sites: The Director of the Agricultural and Mining Department dispatched Inspector Ge Xiaodong to Lishui to inspect the county's forestry sites and the results of spring seedling cultivation and afforestation. He arrived in Lishui by car from Nanjing yesterday and visited County Magistrate Xie and Bureau Chief Zhu of the Finance Bureau the next day to inquire about the economic situation of the site and the local people's concept of forestry. Immediately afterward, Inspector Ge went to the site's forest land and nursery for a week-long inspection. He was quite satisfied with the results of the site's seedling cultivation and Zhongshan Forest. Inspector Ge has prepared a report on the site's situation and will return to the department to report in the near future.

Hangzhou 81

Planned Establishment of Offshore Radio Station: The Zhejiang Provincial Government, considering that the maritime police's anti-bandit and anti-theft operations require speed, plans to establish three radio stations within the jurisdiction of the offshore maritime police bureau to facilitate the transmission of information and benefit defense. If this can be realized, then the suppression of bandits and pirates will be greatly facilitated in the future.

Bandits in the Wenzhou Area Have Been Cleared: The Wenzhou bandit Hu Gongmian, who had more than a thousand followers, occupied Yongjia and other places, falsely claiming to be the Thirteenth Army of the Red Army, with the Wenzhou bandits as the First Corps and the Chuzhou bandits as the Second Corps, and the Yongkang bandits as the Third Corps, with Chen Wencan as the army commander and himself as the director of the political department. The provincial government dispatched land and naval police to attack from all sides, and the two anti-bandit commanders of the four districts, Wang and Gan, repeatedly suppressed them, killing more than two hundred bandits and capturing more than one hundred. The pseudo-army commander Lu Wencan was also captured. The bandit forces have scattered and fled, and the Wenzhou area is as peaceful as ever.

Finance Department Thoroughly Investigates Cumulative Abuses in Unified Tax: The Zhejiang Finance Department, recently, due to poor tax revenue in both regions, and based on numerous petitions from local people to the province, is thoroughly investigating whether it is the bureau director's corruption or the illegality of tax collectors. Yesterday, it secretly appointed Inspector Yao Chong of the department to investigate the cumulative abuses in the Ningbo Foreign and Guangdong Goods and Boat Tax Bureau and ordered the commissioner to formulate rectification measures for future improvement. In addition, in response to a petition from Ningbo citizen Sun Chuo alleging abuses in the Ningbo Cloth Tax, Commissioner Yao was ordered to investigate and reply.

Ningbo 82

Yao Baoweituan Fundraising Committee Member Murdered: Sun Yaoquan, a member of the fundraising committee of the Northeast District Baoweituan in Yuyao, was previously kidnapped by bandits, as detailed in previous reports. It is now heard that after Sun was kidnapped, he was bound with hemp rope by the bandits and a large stone was tied to his back and he was drowned in the Chaotang River. On the 18th of this month, his body floated to the surface of the water. Villagers who saw it reported it to the village committee, which then informed Sun's family to prepare a coffin for burial. It is heard that Sun was generous and righteous and worked hard to suppress bandits and communists, so he incurred the anger of bandit leader Fei Dezhao and others, who sent their henchmen to commit this heinous crime.

Police Chief's Residence Burglarized: The private residence of Mao Binglei, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, in Jiajing Alley in the city was suddenly burglarized at around 1:00 a.m. the night before last. It is heard that a leather suitcase, 150 yuan in cash, and clothing worth more than 400 yuan were stolen. The detective team has been ordered to pursue the case.

Shangyu 83

Two Kidnapping and Robbery Cases Occur in One Night: Wang Chunmao, a resident of Quezuicun, Songxia, west of the county, runs a bamboo yard at home. An elder brother is a businessman in Shanghai. He lives with his younger brother Chunnuan, and both are married. The two brothers usually farm, and their hard work has accumulated some savings, leading to the envy of bandits. On the night of the 19th, around 11:00 p.m., more than twenty pirates broke into the house, searching for property and robbing. When the wives of Mao and Nuan pleaded with the bandits, the bandits took out wooden-cased guns to intimidate them and beat them, causing injuries. Before leaving, the bandits kidnapped both Chunmao and Chunnuan, leaving a note demanding a ransom of 15,000 yuan to be contacted at a certain lane in a certain hotel in Shanghai. They then fired shots and whistled, boarding the Dan boat docked in the back sea and leaving. They released Chunmao midway, telling him to raise the ransom to redeem his younger brother. After the villagers learned of this, they gave chase but were shot back by the bandits. Also on the same night, the Zhang Zhengda Tai Ji Weihuohao, opened by Zhang Aqi in Zhushao Township, was broken into by many pirates who leaped in and robbed silver dollars, hams, and other items worth more than 1,000 yuan.

Beaten to Death for Gonging to Chase Thieves: In Xia Gaishan, a coastal and low-lying area in the northern countryside, seven or eight pirates with sharp blades and pistols came to the home of a farmer surnamed Chen the day before yesterday afternoon and carried away all the utensils and clothing. When a neighbor, A, gonged to wake up the villagers, the bandits, hearing the gong sound, beat A to death before finally going to the beach to board the Dan boat and heading towards Yuyao.

Loss of 5,000 Gold Coins While Watching a Play: Xie Atong of Fangnong Village in the western countryside brought his entire family, young and old, to the neighboring village of Hengting yesterday afternoon to watch a Yangge play. He forgot to properly dispose of the mosquito repellent smoke in the thatched sheep shed, causing the smoke to ignite the hay and burn four new buildings to ashes in an instant. By the time the neighbors discovered the fire and tried to put it out, it was too late. The estimated loss, including rice, was more than 5,000 gold coins.

Education News Highlights

Fourth Day of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society 84

Public Lectures Held and More Than Twenty Matters Resolved

Ma Yinchu Elected President, Actively Raising Funds

The 23rd was the fourth day of the Seventh Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society. The details are recorded below:

Public Lectures: At 9:00 a.m. on the 23rd, public lectures were held at the County Chamber of Commerce, with over a thousand people in attendance. Zhu Bin Yuan presided, and He De Kui spoke on methods to remedy the decline of banks. Li Yunliang spoke on the infringed Chinese shipping industry, and Zhu Qing spoke on communism and the doctrine of loyalty and reciprocity. In the afternoon, they visited a yarn factory. In the evening, a thank-you banquet was held. Due to the death of Tan Yankai, entertainment was canceled.

Society Affairs Meeting: The Society Affairs Meeting was held at 2:00 p.m. on the 22nd, with President Ma Yinchu presiding and Xu Shi Shen recording. After the meeting, President Ma and Secretary Zhu Bin Yuan, Accountant Cai Chengxin, and Quarterly Editor-in-Chief Li Quanshi each reported separately. Accountant Cai Chengxin reported on the foundation's accounting status, stating that most of the foundation raised by the Society had been used to purchase government bonds. The remaining funds were deposited in various banks in Shanghai. Category A funds received 48,000 yuan, and Category B funds spent 29,000 yuan on government bonds. The remaining funds were deposited in the Shanghai Zhejiang Industrial Bank and the Shanghai China Bank, which will soon purchase government bonds and be used in accordance with the foundation's charter.

Resolved Matters: Li Quanshi argued that the allocation of the Society's Sixth Fund should prioritize publishing expenses. After the chairman obtained the consent of the members, it was submitted for discussion and resolved to be handled by the board of directors. The agenda was then discussed item by item. The meeting proceeded as follows: 1. The board of directors proposed that the Society should add sponsoring members. As this involved amending the Society's charter, in accordance with Article 11 of the Society's charter, the charter must be amended with the consent of at least two-thirds of the votes. After the chairman put it to a vote twice, the votes for and against both failed to reach two-thirds, and it was decided to retain the original proposal. 2. The board of directors proposed that membership qualifications should be restricted. Those who have no economic works or have not made contributions to economics studies should not be admitted to the Society. 3. Zhu Bin Yuan proposed that the Society should promote the establishment of branches, and members should be divided into groups to study economic problems to strengthen the spirit of unity and promote academics. All were resolved to be adopted as proposed. 4. Zhu Bin Yuan proposed suggesting that the government quickly establish banking regulations to consolidate the national financial organization. The chairman explained that the National Government's Legislative Yuan has already begun drafting banking laws, and the Society does not seem to need to make further suggestions. The original proposer, Zhu Bin Yuan, stated that he would withdraw the proposal. 5. Li Quanshi proposed that members should strive to make economic science independent and economic books Chinese. It was resolved to be adopted as proposed. 6. Already discussed in advance. 7. Ma Chonggan proposed that the Society should hold more lectures in major ports and publish articles to serve as a reference for society when major economic problems occur in society. 8. Liu Dajun proposed that the chairman of this year's conference should appoint three or five members of the lecture conference committee to consult with members from various places to pre-schedule the lecture conference agenda for the year in various places. The agenda must specify the meeting period, topic of the paper, and the name of the person in charge, and be announced before the general meeting. The above two proposals were resolved to be sent to the board of directors for implementation as originally proposed. 9. Jin Guobao proposed that the Society should promote the development of the Chinese commercial paper market. It was resolved to be adopted as originally proposed. 10. Lin Wei proposed suggesting that the government quickly formulate a national official accounting system. Wei Tingsheng argued that the Ministry of Finance recently organized an accounting committee to improve the accounting system. At the same time, the Central Political Conference also decided to establish a Comptroller Office with separate budget, accounting, and statistics bureaus to rectify revenue and expenditure and improve the accounting system. This proposal does not seem to need to suggest to the government. As a result, it was resolved to publish the original proposal in the Society's quarterly.

Temporary Proposals: Member Gu Tingsheng temporarily proposed that Article 6 of the Society's charter regarding the re-election of directors should be revised and proposed amendments to the charter. After discussion by the public, Article 11 of the charter stipulates that the amendment of the charter must be notified to the members one month before the meeting. The temporary proposal to amend it did not comply with the above provisions. It was resolved that Wei should solicit the endorsement of the members and submit it for discussion and amendment at the next general meeting. Next, Fang Jiaobo, a member of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, was introduced by the chairman.

Fundraising: Next, the chairman reported on the fundraising process of the Society, stating that the Society's fund has raised 40,000 to 50,000 yuan through a year of effort and obtained the assistance of Jin Guobao, a member of the Society and the former director of the Nanjing Special Municipality Finance Bureau, to purchase five acres of official land in the old Wangfu of the capital. The land is located in the center of the capital's banks and large companies and is very important. According to market prices, it should be worth more than 10,000 gold. It is now purchased at an official price of more than 2,000 yuan. However, the Society's fund is scheduled to raise 100,000 yuan, and the current amount is still far from the quota. The speaker believes that members should work together to raise funds and propose methods to follow the methods of the National Tsing Hua University Construction Alumni Association to raise 100 yuan of funds from each graduate, which will be accumulated for six years. Each share of interest is also far from 100 yuan, and the principal will be cleared separately to use the interest for construction. The alumni association is very wealthy and has repaid all the borrowed funds. This is indeed the best way to raise funds that can be used as an example. The Society can also imitate each person to raise 100 yuan each. Those who are willing to recognize more can listen. There are more than 400 members in the entire Society, that is, at least 40,000 yuan can be obtained. If it is profitable for seven years, 40,000 yuan of interest can be obtained. At that time, the principal will be repaid separately, and the interest will be used as the Society's fund. Is it feasible to discuss the results of the public decision to pass all the staff to be implemented by the board of directors

Photography of the Seventh Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society (Taken by Wuxi Mingxing Photo Studio)

Preparing Branches: Finally, the chairman reported that the Society originally had a branch in Shanghai, but because the General Society's board of directors often held meetings in Shanghai, the branch was withdrawn. Now the Hangzhou branch has established a branch due to the large number of members. It seems necessary to restore the organization of the Shanghai branch. After public discussion, it was resolved that one place with more than ten members can write to the General Society to organize a branch; two, the General Society should be stationed in Nanjing, and the Council of the General Society should stipulate that meetings should be held in Beijing; three, the Shanghai branch should actively seek a location and restore the organization.

Next Annual Meeting: Next, the chairman proposed again to discuss and decide the location of the eighth annual meeting to be held next year. After the public expressed their opinions one after another, the following six locations were proposed by each member: Hangzhou, Ningbo, Table Island, Liaoning, Beiping, and Suzhou. The board of directors will consider the situation and select one place as the venue for the next annual meeting.

Elected Directors: The results of the elected directors were announced as follows: President Ma Yinchu, Vice President Liu Dajun, Directors Zhu Bin Yuan, Li Quanshi, Wei Tingsheng, Pan Xulun, Jin Guobao, Xu Jizhi, Liu Binglin

Group Reception: On the 22nd, seven groups, including the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce, silk, yarn, flour, silver, and dyeing groups, hired five boats and four sailing boats to entertain all the members to visit Meiyuan, Xiaojishan, Yuantouzhu, Jichang Garden, and Huangbudun. They enjoyed a banquet on the boat from 8:00 a.m. to 9:30 p.m. before returning.

The Process of Taking Office in Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools 85

The principals of Jiangsu Provincial Middle Schools took the opportunity to go to the province to swear an oath of office. In advance, they gathered at Zhen Middle School to hold a principals' meeting to discuss funding and other issues. At first, they were unwilling to take the oath, which ultimately led to obedience. This has already been reported in this newspaper. The twists and turns before taking office this time are roughly recorded as follows: After the middle school principals arrived in the province on the 20th, they held a meeting at Zhen Middle School on the same day. Most of the principals believed that they had served as principals for several years and had taken oaths of office in the past. Administrative authorities should separately stipulate dates and send personnel to each school to swear an oath and give speeches to show solemnity. This gathering in the province to hold the ceremony is an innovation that is quite boring and only wastes time and travel expenses. But since they have come, they may as well do as usual, so the first day's meeting decided to resign collectively to the Department of Education after the inauguration ceremony. During the second meeting on the afternoon of the 21st, it was felt that it was too ridiculous to take office first and then resign, and because of excessive arrears in funding, it was difficult for each school to maintain itself. The Department of Education also "hired" the principals as "directors" (and the headmaster of Suxu Middle School was arrested for no reason) and the rights of the principals of the provincial middle schools were too unprotected. Therefore, Zhou Xingbei, Zheng Xigu, Wang Xiacai, and Ren Zhongmin were elected as representatives to go to the Department of Education to seek a delay in holding the oath of office ceremony. Chen and Yao, two members of the Department, agreed to convey this to the director. That night, Chen Hexian returned to Zhen and learned of the principals' meeting. He immediately summoned Wang Xiacai and Ren Zhongmin to his residence for a conversation. Chen told Wang that the oath of office ceremony in the Department had already been prepared and could not be stopped. As for the funding and assistance to the headmaster of Suxu Middle School who was arrested, the Department of Education would do its best to do so. Wang then conveyed this intention to the principals. As a result, the opinions of the middle school principals suddenly diverged. Some insisted on complying with the resolution and resolutely postponing the inauguration for the sake of preserving the resolution and the principals' credibility. Others said that the resolution was to ask four representatives to go to the Department of Education to negotiate a postponement, not not to hold it. Now that the Department of Education has difficulties, it is natural to still comply with the Department of Education's notice and go to the Department on time to take the oath. Some had no opinion at all and were good at observing the situation. Their attitude was neutral. The middle school principals' meeting was divided into four, which was difficult to continue. Finally, it was decided to hold another meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 22nd before going to the Department to take office, and to review the resolution of the previous day. As for the elementary school principals' meeting, the issue of taking office was not discussed when it was held on the 21st. Upon learning of this divergent opinion on the middle school side, the elementary school principals gathered all the principals at the Zhen Middle School Elementary School at 8:30 a.m. yesterday (the 22nd) to discuss the results of the discussion and sent a letter to the Middle School Principals' Association. The original letter stated that the elementary school's collective discussion decided to act in concert with the middle school. The joint meeting of middle and elementary school principals (the middle school principals had the idea of holding a joint meeting with the elementary school principals on the evening of the 21st) seems unnecessary. Please show the middle school principal's record of the day's decision. At the same time, all the elementary school principals waited quietly for the middle school principals' reply at Zhen Middle School Elementary School in order to act in concert. At 10:30 a.m., they received a reply from Zhou Xingbei, chairman of the Middle School Principals' Association, stating that the middle school principals had unanimously decided to go to the Department of Education to take the oath of office immediately. The elementary school principals had no preconceived notions about this, only looking to the middle school principals for guidance and immediately went to the Department to take the oath of office. Most of the middle school principals who initially advocated postponing the inauguration had already arrived at the Department. This is the process before the principals took office.

Zhejiang Department of Education Investigates Party Member Activities in Various Schools 87

Education Society Hangzhou News: The Zhejiang Department of Education recently wants to understand the number of party members and their activities in various schools in the province in order to implement party ideology education for reference. It has specially created and issued two types of investigation forms: the Party Member Investigation Form and the Party Affairs Investigation Form, and ordered the city governments and provincial middle schools in various counties to fill them out for filing and reference. The content is as follows: (A) Party Member Investigation Form 1. Name 2. Age 3. Place of Origin 4. Party Experience 5. Date of Joining the Party 6. Date of Last Registration 7. Party Certificate Number 8. Current District Branch 9. Remarks (Fill in whether you are a teacher, staff member, or student and whether you are currently an official of the Party Department) (B) Party Affairs Investigation Form 1. School Name 2. Number of teachers and staff who are party members 3. Number of students who are party members 4. Party organization in the school (Fill in the name of the school and whether there is a district branch or district party department. If there is an organization, fill in the name, number of party members, and the lives of the staff in detail) 5. Party activities in the school (Fill in the details of party members' meetings, small-scale activities, and other situations regarding party activities)

Wuxian Training Department Reviews Boy Scouts on National Day 88

The Wuxian Training Department specially convened all group leaders and service members in the county yesterday to hold a conversation to explain the significance of this review and the points to be noted during the review. More than ten people, including Jin Weizheng, attended. Chairman Yang Shengzu reported on the work of the Training Department for the Boy Scouts in the past: (1) The Board of Directors is preparing and will be established soon (2) The registration of Boy Scouts and service members will continue (3) The Department will hold a grand review on National Day to encourage children's ability to do things and to enable the public to understand the Boy Scout cause. It is hoped that all comrades will step up training. It is also heard that the number of people participating in each group is about 700. The following regulations are also specified: 1. Local

Temporary Elementary School Registration Deadline Ends 89

Ends at the end of this month

New teachers hired by municipal elementary schools in Shanghai should be qualified registrants. The Municipal Bureau of Education fears that various schools are hiring teachers indiscriminately, so it implemented temporary registration before the start of school. It has been three months and should end now. The Bureau has now announced that those who have already registered and submitted certificates but have not passed the oral examination, and those who have already registered and passed but have not yet claimed their certificates, etc., must come to the Bureau to collect them before the end of this month. Do not make a mistake.

Unregistered Rural Schools to Lose Subsidies 90

Prior to the separation of the city and county of Shanghai, many private schools in rural areas were subsidized by the county education bureau, nominally as substitute elementary schools. After the municipal government took over, this practice continued. The municipal education bureau has now found that the private school subsidy regulations stipulate that only private schools that have been approved for registration can apply for subsidies. As these substitute elementary schools have not applied for registration in accordance with private school regulations, all originally issued subsidies should be stopped to comply with regulations. It is reported that all schools have been notified to stop subsidies immediately.

County Education Bureau Re-Divides County School Districts 91

The schools in the six districts of Shanghai County were originally divided by the County Education Bureau into three school districts, each assigned with one supervisor and two education committee members for rotational inspection. The bureau now considers this approach to be inadequate and has decided to change it from this year onward to eastern and western districts. Districts one, three, and six (formerly the four townships of Minhang, Beiqiao, Maqiao) will be the western school district, while districts two, four, and five (formerly the three townships of Tangwan, Sanlin, Chenxing) will be the eastern school district. However, since each school district has too many schools, making thorough inspections difficult, it is planned that the central school districts will distribute schools, and the central school principals will be responsible for inspections, which will be submitted to the bureau for review. All administrative responsibilities will still be borne by the education committee members.

Opening of Public Schools in the County 92

Public schools under Shanghai County have been prepared by the County Education Bureau. The school is located inside the county government. Teachers are assigned by the party headquarters, the county government, and various bureaus. In recent days, public servants from various agencies have been actively registering. The official opening ceremony was held last night (the 22nd).

Overseas Teachers Recruited by the Vocational Guidance Institute 93

Since the establishment of the Nanyang Vocational Introduction Department of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute, it has received commissions from educational and cultural institutions in various ports of Nanyang to find male and female teachers. Recently, Ms. Li was introduced as a teacher at a school in Java and will soon depart. Yesterday, the institute received a commission from a Chinese school in Jakarta to recruit an elementary school teaching director. The requirements are graduation from a university education department, ability to teach Mandarin, teaching experience in education, and interest in elementary school education. The monthly salary is 61 guilders (equivalent to 100 Chinese dollars), with board and lodging provided, and approximately 100 dollars for travel expenses. Those interested can inquire about their resumes at the overseas vocational introduction department of the society.
